{

  else CountPositive(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] > 0 then 1 else 0)
}

{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)

  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)

{

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)

  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
  assert pcount == CountPositive(a[..n]) + 0; // ensures pcount holds the count of positives
  assert ncount == CountNegative(a[..n]) + 0; // ensures ncount holds the count of negatives

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{

    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)

{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' :: d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }

  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])

  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])

  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;

    i := i + 1;

  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else CountNegative(a[..|a|-1]) + (if a[|a|-1] < 0 then 1 else 0)
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    assert d != 0;
    CountPosDivPos(a, d);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert d != 0;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, d);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, -1) == CountNegative(a); // lemma proves this
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a); // lemma proves this
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a); // lemma proves this
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
}

  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|

  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{

    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := (n + 1) / 2;
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    // For each non‑zero divisor d', the number of positives after division is
    // strictly less than half the length of a.  We prove this by case analysis
    // on the sign of d'.
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
        // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a)
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountPositive(a);
        // Since pcount < half, CountPositive(a) < half
        assert CountPositive(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) <=>
          pcount < half;
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|);
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
        // CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a)
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') == CountNegative(a);
        // Since ncount < half, CountNegative(a) < half
        assert CountNegative(a) < CeilHalf(|a|) <=>
          ncount < half;
        assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|);
      }
    }
  }

lemma CountPosDivPos(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d > 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivPos(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
  assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountPositive(a);
}

lemma CountPosDivNeg(a: seq<int>, d: int)
  requires d < 0
  ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a)
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| > 0 {
    CountPosDivNeg(a[..|a|-1], d);
  }
  assert CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) == CountNegative(a);
}

method BePositive(a: seq<int>) returns (d: int)
  ensures d != 0 ==> -1000 <= d <= 1000
                      && CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|)
  ensures d == 0 ==> (forall d' :: d' == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|))
{
  var n := |a|;
  var pcount := 0;
  var ncount := 0;
  var zcount := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant pcount == CountPositive(a[..i])
    invariant ncount == CountNegative(a[..i])
    invariant zcount == CountPositive(a[..i]) + CountNegative(a[..i]) - i
  {
    if a[i] > 0 {
      pcount := pcount + 1;
    } else if a[i] < 0 {
      ncount := ncount + 1;
    } else {
      zcount := zcount + 1;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  var half := CeilHalf(n);
  if pcount >= half {
    d := 1;
    CountPosDivPos(a, 1);
  } else if ncount >= half {
    d := -1;
    CountPosDivNeg(a, -1);
  } else {
    d := 0;
    forall d' | d' != 0
      ensures CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d') < CeilHalf(|a|)
    {
      if d' > 0 {
        CountPosDivPos(a, d');
      } else {
        CountPosDivNeg(a, d');
      }
    }
  }
  assert d == 0 || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) >= CeilHalf(|a|) || CountPositiveAfterDiv(a, d) < CeilHalf(|a|);
}
